Krish is the son of a billionaire businessman. He has a girlfriend Indu. Her friend Bhoomi wants to pursue her higher studies and lands in trouble when her father wants to marry her to his nephew. Her grandfather convinces her dad, saying that she already likes someone in the city so her dad asks her to bring her lover home. Indu asks Krish to go as Bhoomi's Lover. Meanwhile, Bhoomi's uncle, and her father live apart in two adjacent villages. The two families are feuding with each other. Krish is hated by Bhoomi's entire family and he has to overcome many things in his attempt to get everyone to love him.Krish is the son of a billionaire businessman. He has a girlfriend Indu. Jesus said, â€œExcept ye repent, ye shall all likewise perishâ€ (Luke 13:3,5).  â€œRepentâ€ means to have a change of mind that results in a change of heart and a change of direction.  It is like making a u-turn on the highway.  Repentance is saying, â€œI donâ€™t like the road Iâ€™m on.  I donâ€™t like the direction Iâ€™m headed.  I sure donâ€™t like where this road is taking me.â€  YOU MUST RECEIVE Jesus as your Savior. To â€œreceiveâ€ Jesus means to place your faith in Him.  All you have to do is accept Jesus and confess Him as your personal Savior and Lord.  HERE IS A SUGGESTED PRAYER.  Please know that there is nothing magical about praying words that you do not mean.  But, if these words express what you would like to say to God, pray this prayer from the depths of your heart:  â€œDear Lord Jesus, thank you for loving me.  I believe that you are Godâ€™s Son.
